<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>боль</a> (536)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>боль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bolь</i>.

(<a href = vnd.unilang:мед.html>мед</a>.) <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> 8e: мн. ч. — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>бо́ли</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>боле́й</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>боля́м</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>боля́ми</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>боля́х</a></i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:больничный.html>больни́чный</a> (6640)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больница.html>больни́ца</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolʹníca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больничный.html>больни́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bolʹníčnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hospital</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больничный.html>больни́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bolʹníčnyj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больничный.html>больни́чного</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> medical certificate, sick list</li>
<li>sick leave</li></ol>

***больно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:больно.html>больно</a> (1497)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolʹnój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больно.html>бо́льно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bólʹno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bad, badly</li>
<li>painfully</li>
<li>extremely, terribly</li>
<li>a bit too</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больно.html>больно́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bolʹnó</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolʹnój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>бо́ль</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a>, определительное, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> предикатив; неизменяемое. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — больнее, больней.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-боль-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-н-о</b>.
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>боль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ной</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-noj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bolʹnój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)больне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)больне́й</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sick, ill</li>
<li>painful</li>
<li>weak</li>
<li>morbid</li></ol>

***большак.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:большак.html>больша́к</a> (22080)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:большак.html>больша́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bolʹšák</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:большак.html>большака́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:большак.html>большаки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:большак.html>большако́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a large road in rural areas</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> male head of a family</li></ol>

***большевистский.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:большевистский.html>большеви́стский</a> (10013)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From an ephemeral <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">большеви́ст</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolʹševíst</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> which has however reached persistent prominency in other languages as <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bolschewist</i>. While the form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:большевистский.html>большеви́стский</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolʹševístskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> has, with help by the Soviet ruling class, attained exclusivity, the exiled enemies of the reds – including in Germany – have continued to use the form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">большеви́цкий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolʹševíckij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, regularly derived from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:большевик.html>большеви́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolʹševík</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>боль</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ше<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ви́ст<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ский</b>

</p>
<ol><li>bigger, greater (comparative degree of <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bolʹšój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:великий.html>вели́кий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">velíkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>)</li></ol>

***большой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́й</a> (62)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bel-</i>, whence Ancient Greek <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">βελτῐ́ων</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">beltíōn</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">better</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болячка.html>боля́чка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">boljáčka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болячка.html>боля́чки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болячка.html>боля́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болячка.html>боля́чек</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бомбардировка.html>бомбардиро́вка</a> (16427)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бомбардирова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bombardirovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бомбардировка.html>бомбардиро́вка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bombardiróvka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бомбардировка.html>бомбардиро́вки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бомбардировка.html>бомбардиро́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бомбардировка.html>бомбардиро́вок</a></b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бомбить.html>бомби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bombítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбомбить.html>разбомби́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bomb</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to provide private taxi services without a license</li></ol>

***бомж.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бомж.html>бомж</a> (9359)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Acronym of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a> <b>б</b>ез <b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></b>пределённого <b>м</b>е́ста <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>ж</a></b>и́тельства</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">licó <b>b</b>ez <b>o</b>predeljónnovo <b>m</b>ésta <b>ž</b>ítelʹstva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> - a person without defined place of residence.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бомж.html>бомж</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bomž</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бомж.html>бомжа́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бомж.html>бомжи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бомж.html>бомже́й</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">бомжи́ха</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tramp, bum, hobo, slacker, homeless person</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> poorly dressed person
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>Из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приличный.html>прили́чной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:семья.html>семьи́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>хо́дит</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бомж.html>бомжо́м</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Iz prilíčnoj semʹí, a xódit <b>bomžóm</b>!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He’s from a decent family, but dresses like a bum!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***бон.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бон.html>бон</a> (14112)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">bon</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бон.html>бон</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bon</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бон.html>бо́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бон.html>бо́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бон.html>бо́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>voucher</li>
<li>bon (an early type of paper currency)</li>
<li>any paper currency collected by notaphilists</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">бони́ст</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">boníst</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">бони́стика</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bonístika</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Shortening of <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">бонхе́д</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bonxéd</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bonehead</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бон.html>бон</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bon</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бон.html>бо́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бон.html>бо́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бон.html>бо́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a Neo-Nazi skinhead</li></ol>

***бор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бор.html>бор</a> (9437)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">bore</i> or from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:бор.html>Bor</a></i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бордель.html>борде́ль</a> (15705)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bordell</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">bordel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bordellum</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бордель.html>борде́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bordɛ́lʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бордель.html>борде́ля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бордель.html>борде́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бордель.html>борде́лей</a></b>)

</p>

</p>
<ol><li>Bordeaux <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">type of wine</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:борец.html>боре́ц</a> (7150)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*borьcь</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*borti</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ьcь</i>; synchronically derivable from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">боро́ть(ся)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">borótʹ(sja)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ц</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-éc</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борец.html>боре́ц</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">boréc</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борец.html>борца́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борец.html>борцы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борец.html>борцо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fighter, champion</li>
<li>wrestler</li>
<li>monkshood, wolfsbane, aconitum</li></ol>

***боржоми.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:боржоми.html>боржо́ми</a> (26656)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Georgian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Georgian language">Georgian</a></span> <i class="Geor mention" lang="ka">ბორჯომი</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ka-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">borǯomi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боржоми.html>боржо́ми</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">boržómi</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Borjomi (a brand, well-known in the USSR, of naturally carbonated mineral water from Georgia (country)).</li></ol>
